\definecolor{drawColor}{RGB}{0,0,0}

\path[draw=drawColor,line width= 0.4pt,dash pattern=on 4pt off 4pt ,line join=round,line cap=round] (402.52, 52.80) -- (402.52,246.35);
\end{scope}
\end{tikzpicture}
